, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Hinduism , the oldest religion -- is a just way of managing life. &nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Bhagavad Gita is all about BEING IN THE MOMENT.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Man is the only living creature who can control or change his life. He is not a slave to his surroundings or at the mercy of nature.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Knowledge is the only weapon which follows the owner everywhere.&nbsp; Knowledge has to b</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">e challenged and improved constantly</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Man</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"> has 3 sides to his nature \u2013body, mind and spirit . A proper balance between the 3 is desired. If any of the 3 is undeveloped he will suffer in life. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Life is a combination or physical, intellectual and spiritual aspects. Without spiritual development , man is without love or positive emotions ( affection, care, respect, sympathy ) .&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Effective life management means creating an equilibrium \u2013</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"> </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">in short success.&nbsp; Without positive emotions man cant be happy. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">A wise man can live in peace with things he cannot change. Never try to do things you cant</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">.</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"> What is the point in teaching a donkey to sing. It is a sheer waste of time and effort. A student who has failed must not blame the question paper or examiner. He was not prepared. Be prepared\u2014win some , lose some\u2014but at least you tried.</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Nature follows the law, use it or lose it.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">There is this famous yogi &nbsp;who went into severe penance for 20 years by standing on one leg and keeping one hand lifted up. By the time he finished his lifted up hand had shrivelled .</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">You must fight and make your own life on the planet. Don\u2019t expect anybody else to do it for you.&nbsp; Make most of the best and least of the worst. Man alone is the architect of his destiny.&nbsp; Inaction is worse than no action at all.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">No dream can become true unless you have some skill and go to work. Check out what skills are most needed in the market.&nbsp; Choose a job you love, then you don\u2019t have to work a day in your life. Hunt or get hunted.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Belief is the power behind all accomplishments. The man who wins is the man who thinks he can.&nbsp; Faith and trust are the seeds which bring the sweet fruits of success. Faith is about \u201c can do\u201d&nbsp; think \u201c it is possible\u201d&nbsp; it gives you new energy. Faith is the bird which sings when the dawn is still dark. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Will power is the decision to carry on the fight. Self esteem is required to make a person mentally healthy. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Friendship is like a plant \u2013it must be watered and nurtured. Emotional health cannot be grown alone. Man is a social animal. We need family and friends to improve our emotional health. No one can lead a healthy life in isolation. Acceptance between man and society must be 2 way. Society will accept you if you follow the norms and when you are of some use to others. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">A mentally healthy person learns to evaluate himself , his own performance and behaviour. An unusual amount of commonsense is called wisdom. Wisdom is discriminating between right and wrong. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Knowledge is about knowing more and more\u2014WISDOM IS ABOUT KNOWING &nbsp;LESS AND LESS . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">To be successful you must be exited about life. Life is a festival only to those who live with enthusiasm.&nbsp; Lack of enthusiasm wrinkles the soul.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Try to see a situation as it is from different angles and not as you want. If your life is free of opportunities then you are not taking enough risks. If you want peace you must be prepared for war. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;Only an asshole will </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;start di</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">g</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">ging a well</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">, when he gets thirsty.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAbkaQ7yeI/AAAAAAAAA2o/MoZILWQQKCI/s1600/imagesCASABJ6X.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAbkaQ7yeI/AAAAAAAAA2o/MoZILWQQKCI/s1600/imagesCASABJ6X.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">It is not enough to aim, you must hit. Failure to hit the bulls eye is never the fault of the target. You have to choose your own goal, at the same time follow social norms. Belief in predetermined destiny is the only refuge of weak minds. Take responsibility for your failures.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Self respect commands respect from others.&nbsp; If you don\u2019t know simply say so. Frankness does not require being brutally so.&nbsp; True salesmanship starts when the customer says NO.&nbsp; A kite rises only against the wind. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAbtvmhGYI/AAAAAAAAA2s/Rtw7Kd3mhHY/s1600/imagesCAMXQATA.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAbtvmhGYI/AAAAAAAAA2s/Rtw7Kd3mhHY/s1600/imagesCAMXQATA.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Remove all ugly looking things from your surroundings.. Avoid people whom you don\u2019t like. Don\u2019t discuss topics you don\u2019t relish. Don\u2019t think about people whom you don\u2019t like. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Good manners are the best letters of recommendation.&nbsp; Bad manners reduce our acceptability in society, thereby affecting our social relations. A good laugh is the best medicine.. &nbsp;</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">L</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">aughter is a tranquiliser with no side effects.&nbsp; Laughter is the cheapest luxury, it electrifies the nerves and cleanse the system. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Prayer renews our internal strength during rough weather. A prayer is to the soul what air is to the lungs. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">( take this form a hardcore sailor who has never said a prayer in his life \u2013even when his ship was 35 miles off super typhoon Bart at 925 mb atmospheric pressure and 225 knots of wind ). After studying Quantum physics I do feel nowadays that Prayer is powerful.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Better a thousand enemies outside the house than one inside.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Carelessness can do more harm than lack of knowledge. It should not become a habit. If carelessness is not trying to know the destructive forces, negligence is overlooking the destructive forces. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">There is nothing that wastes the body and mind like worry. Worries are more about yesterday and tomorrow. Don\u2019t take tomorrow to bed with you.&nbsp; There is a difference between planning and worrying. Planning is constructive, worry is destructive.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Try to forget useless things. To remember everything is to make your mind a dustbin.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Love is food for the soul. Jealousy is poison for the soul.&nbsp; Better to forgive and forget than hate and remember. Fear tends to produce the things we are afraid of. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">The greatest wealth is contentment with little. It consists in simple wants.&nbsp; Try to live slightly below your means.&nbsp; </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">Too much glamour is like too much spices. It harms. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">The blatant display of status symbols </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">is the result of low self esteem. The self confident person can afford to project a modest image. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">It is better to aim at a good thing and miss than to aim at a bad thing and hit. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">The best time to solve a problem is as soon at it happens. Reward yourself every time you achieve success. It pays to rew</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">a</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">rd yourself. It give give a boost to your zeal to achieve the next goal.</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">No process takes place without a principle. Principle is the cause and process is the effect.&nbsp; Principles are fair and impartial to all, incl the non living things at all place and time. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">WE CANNOT CREATE OR DESTROY THE ENERGY OR MATTER IN THE UNIVERSE. BUT WE CAN SURELY CHANGE ITS FORM. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">You cannot change your past, you cannot survive without water, you cannot change natures principle. The only solution is to accept things as they are. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">No single agency can make a process happen. A process happens when at lest 2 agencies play a complimentary role. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , sans-serif;\">Life is a grindstone </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">--</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"> whether is powders you to dust or polishes you depends on what you are made of. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">The purpose of life is not only to be happy, but also to be creative , productive and useful\u2014to make a difference that you lived at all on this planet.&nbsp; There is no experience better for the heart than to reach down and lift people. </span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif;\">The smallest good deed is better than the grandest good attention. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\nYou have to bring meaning to your own life a painting or a song-- a celebration NOT a competition. &nbsp;Real richness consists of a singing heart-- Seriousness is a disease.<br />\n<br />\n-- NOT a Donald Trump type money arrogant character ( and there are so many richer people that him on this planet- he and his side kicks must be surely under severe delusion !).<br />\n<br />\nSuch ugly rich people can shout \" You are Fired!\" -- &nbsp;deep inside he is a joyless and unloved beggar. There is no beauty , grace and peace. He can try to create grace with money -- but alas , grace is spiritual and comes as a flowering of your being. Life cannot be event managed.<br />\n<br />\nOnly people with inferiority complex wants to impress others. What matters is how you played the game--not whether you lost or won-- or was fired!<br />\n<br />\nDo not go around copying others signatures. All imitations are plastic. There is great joy in being ordinary. Live life a bit hot, burn the torch at both ends , throw all the paint you can on the canvas of life-- but your innermost core must be cool.<br />\n<br />\nNever fall into the same hole twice. The first fall can be deemed as experience. Only what you experience is yours.<br />\n<br />\nTruth blossoms only in individual freedom. It can never happen to a crowd. If you surrender your freedom and individuality big brother and the society will give you great posts and respectability. Dare to be who you are.<br />\n<br />\nYou are responsible only to yourself. No order is higher than your own intelligence.<br />\n<br />\nCreating guilt in you is the oldest trick of all religions. A happy person carries his own temple around him. Repressed sexuality causes almost all diseases.A man of awareness never reacts and so is unpredictable.<br />\n<br />\nEliminate the needless wants of life. Never feel shy to show feelings.<br />\n<br />\nYou must allow life its freedom. All perfectionism is a deep ego trip. Never betray a trust. &nbsp;Get along with people. Use soft words and hard arguments . Laugh, have fun. Most of your pain is self chosen.<br />\n<br />\nYou are in this river of life only for a short time on a raft--very soon 100% , you will plunge down the waterfall and die. &nbsp;Enjoy the fish you caught--don't&nbsp;keep fishing like a moron --for you cant take it all to your grave. Don't be in awe of death and demean life on the &nbsp;raft.&nbsp;YOU CANT BANISH THE DANGERS , BUT YOU CAN BANISH YOUR FEARS.<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; line-height: 14px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; line-height: 14px;\">You have succeeded in life when all you really want is only what you really need.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 14px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">YOU ARE NEVER A LOSER UNLESS YOU QUIT TRYING.!&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;\">One day you find, 10 years have got behind you. No one told you when to run, you missed the starting gun. - Pink Floyd</span></i><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAa9FP3TgI/AAAAAAAAA2c/VzZ5I0593TU/s1600/imagesCA4X3IMT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAa9FP3TgI/AAAAAAAAA2c/VzZ5I0593TU/s1600/imagesCA4X3IMT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c565312184603740998\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_150M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/02953946768225924434\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">TV</a></cite><span class=\"icon user\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/06/the-deep-state-and-shadow-government_13.html?showComment=1529055108183#c565312184603740998\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">June 15, 2018 at 3:01 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_150MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nShri Ajit Vadakayil, my colleague Sachveer earlier contacted you. "published": "2010-11-27T00:47:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-11-30T09:16:58+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkxMDg4ODE4MTg1Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/11/virtual-teaming-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8193875144415239426", "title": "VIRTUAL TEAMING --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "VIRTUAL TEAMING -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEe75J3EI/AAAAAAAAA08/h0pzTHH3uQE/s1600/capt_ajit_vadakayil_3.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEe75J3EI/AAAAAAAAA08/h0pzTHH3uQE/s1600/capt_ajit_vadakayil_3.JPG\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEsjvfMWI/AAAAAAAAA1A/jWEGDLAPGDQ/s1600/imagesCAR1L1Y6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEsjvfMWI/AAAAAAAAA1A/jWEGDLAPGDQ/s1600/imagesCAR1L1Y6.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEv78y_2I/AAAAAAAAA1E/-I7grxyrAEg/s1600/vt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAEv78y_2I/AAAAAAAAA1E/-I7grxyrAEg/s1600/vt.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nthis 21st century has just begun and lot of companies are boasting of their flat organisational structures (with hierarchy still deeply entrenched!). <br />\n<br />\nin my vision for the next century i see the need for the management structure to be perfect like the nervous system of the human body\u2014<br />\n<br />\nthis is the ultimate form of management as the human body is the most complex structure you can ever imagine\u2014what could be more complex that the micro-science of human senses or DNA ? <br />\n<br />\nwe now move from flat to unreal structures ( patience ulysses! , i will explain your tool value later ) -- or for the matter virtual teaming.<br />\n<br />\na virtual team ensures the best minds work on a project from their unique vantage points regardless of where they reside and they are all afforded a level field.<br />\n<br />\nbrilliant minds do not care to play on a tilted playing field\u2014whether to their advantage or not. it is realised that sometimes difficult topics are not best addressed face to face as in a office meeting. the member ship of the virtual team is dynamic, it shifts in response to changing project needs as usual in ship management. <br />\n<br />\nbefore i proceed further let me recapitulate what a ordinary team is\u2014individuals in a team share a common goal ( like a football team ) and depend on one another to achieve that goal. nothing can be achieved individually\u2014no one man show is possible. <br />\n<br />\nin this technologically switched on , modern age , it is impossible to get highly qualified people under one roof especially if they are not financially vulnerable and if they are loathe to sacrifice their personal values and private lives. these people of high autonomy and self direction may be unwilling to uproot and relocate their family . for their priorities might be in their children's education or family happiness . or maybe they do not care for the all too familiar dog eat dog office politics\u2014i will come back to this later as a DC . <br />\n<br />\nthis nonsense of location restriction in a high tech age is done away with. virtual teaming affords them the much needed flexibility of balancing their personal and professional lives. any team LOVES to work with people having expertise in their own field. they have the opportunity to leverage others\u2019 expertise in pursuit of team goals and use each other effectively. <br />\n<br />\nmodern technology enables the best committed minds to come together where ever roof they reside. teaming opportunity exists under different roofs all working towards a common goal. communication technologies like email , mobile phones are used instead of visual eye contact. when you can have your laptop and mobile hooked on even on an airplane \u2013work goes where the employee goes. what cannot be conveyed by a nokia mobile N95 digital dvd movie sent by attachment on a email. it is now possible for on the spot member to be part of a virtual team. how many masters have a superintendent tell him by telex\u2014you are the man on the spot\u2014yet strangely he was not part of any vital decision making team\u2014the man on the spot was just a feed back machine for a decision maker who was less competent and had NIL experience on that strain.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAG10l4IPI/AAAAAAAAA1Q/r6iQ9PLpW80/s1600/imagesCAWLZWFS.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPAG10l4IPI/AAAAAAAAA1Q/r6iQ9PLpW80/s1600/imagesCAWLZWFS.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\ndecentralized decision making enables us to focus jointly on work objectives, mutual problems and to develop innovative and effective solutions . cross organisational teamwork creates enormous savings starting from less central office space`and less travel time and costs. <br />\n<br />\nmost of the time the people sitting in the central office space is unaware of the detrimental effects of the things they do or decide on ( to make their own lives simpler ) the others doing the actual job in a far flung place and difficult environment. <br />\n<br />\nwe are lucky to be born in this era of change. since the wheel has been invented maximum changes have happened in our lifetime. this change has to be managed, information is the most powerful tool . this is where a catalysing multipoint feedback from a virtual team comes in handy. this \u201cto the point information\u201d is more powerful than all the voluminous and vague information on the internet superhighway (where time management takes a backseat). virtual teaming causing 360 degrees feedback ( aaha a new buzzword eh? ) creates an environment that allows change management to flourish.<br />\n<br />\nwhen i was on sichem pace it was usual for me to comment /advise or even decide on problems of fairchem colt and north vessels\u2014the idea is to gain quick access to my on the spot experience\u2014the delay of re-inventing the wheel is thus avoided. it was usual for me to help a young master make a maiden entry into the amazon at night or even to comment on a delicate shipboard problems while i was on leave. <br />\n<br />\naccelerated learning and knowledge sharing is the result when you have the maturity to have the team as the unit of performance. i my case i was tightly affiliated with the concerned superintendents\u2014but this is not necessary. sharing databases does not need tight affiliations as long as the prior human trusting and open relation ships have been there. imagine the increased knowledge base when you have instant and ready access to experiences of others \u2013especially in the chemical field. <br />\n<br />\nin my piece on time management i spoke of the need to save time and money by decrease in travel\u2014this is made possible by virtual teaming. communications and feedback are mostly in writing which makes documentation and retrieval easy as long as the email subject header is taken care of. persuasion is through written words than though mannerisms with adequate time for reflection. in a real meeting 80% of what is said is forgotten in 24 hours\u2014things retained in external memory like yesterdays draft or yesterdays forepeak tank sounding.<br />\n<br />\ntraditional teams under one rood interact in meetings\u2014unless this meeting is well conducted there are many pitfalls. office politics play a major role. i will be penning a short para on meetings and office politics in this piece.<br />\n<br />\nin virtual teaming trust ,SYNERGY and sense of belonging is essential\u2014the people under different roofs must be able to count on each other to share information quickly and completely. this trust is more important as virtual teaming eliminates tone of voice, eye contact and body language\u2014the trust indicators. <br />\n<br />\nvirtual team members are highly interdependent\u2014contrary to what the general feeling may be. yet paradoxically the team is diverse \u2013made of individuals excelling in problem solving and innovation. unity is strength provided all are pulling in the same direction. <br />\n<br />\nthe team members must have a commitment never to allow the baby to get burnt. all must appreciate the experience and skills each member can bring to the team. a member is there for what he can contribute ( that leaves out cooks , right? ). members can brainstorm each other with cc and bcc by email to the relevant rest of the team. the copied to members can add to the feedback database. so it goes without saying that the virtual team members must be excellent communicators and must be given the communication mantras.<br />\n<br />\nall the virtual team requires is a good strong respected leader who need not reside necessarily in the central office space . the leader must establish a process for storing and retrieving team members knowledge and work experiences. the leader must be aware of the difference in perspectives and work practises or even styles ( which are confused often with bad intent \u2013remember bad boy vadakayil ?)\u2014<br />\n<br />\nthe leader clarifies the role each individual will play in accomplishing virtual team tasks. the eye must be told to see and not to hear\u2014a small definition of accountability. he must demonstrate an awareness of the challenges others face in their work. autonomy to execute work details is desirable. he encourages open discussions with key players before making a significant decision or policy shift. a frank question say \u201cam i missing something you feel is important? \u201c<br />\n<br />\nthe leader is a misfit if he has a problem in unlearning outdated ways\u2014remember we are in the era of change management\u2014dog eared ledgers are out\u2014microchips are in. the leader encourages the virtual team to take initiative , be self starters and be future focused. he honestly seeks the input of the virtual team to build strategies and action plans. <br />\n<br />\nthe team is no dirty dozen rubbing shoulders with each other. team members must desist from making judgements bases on their own perceptions and history. often the least obvious perspective will bring the most valuable idea or probable solution. so this means each perspective must be encouraged. <br />\n<br />\nso let us imagine the perspectives offered by a virtual team consisting of a kiss guy ( keep it short and simple ), philanthropist, a scientist, a risk taker, a strategist, a visionary, our own good old establishment, a fact finder and a random virtual team member.<br />\n<br />\nwhy were the bridge wing doors shut?<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPRzqBjunXI/AAAAAAAABJA/1KDna9c2ORg/s1600/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPRzqBjunXI/AAAAAAAABJA/1KDna9c2ORg/s1600/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nas you can see , the virtual team member has a trigger mindset. he does care for going through the motions like the others and thinks out of the box. one good idea often triggers another. he encourages each person to express positive and negative feelings. the focus is on creativity, innovation , conflict resolution , sharing/ seeking and harvesting information and to fine tune ideas for better decision making. he believes firmly that everybody must be self directed and flexible in order to work creatively together.<br />\n<br />\nthe virtual team leader realises that brainstorming is a process which must not have knee jerk reactions.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPRwX-tW8VI/AAAAAAAABIc/lepwVpxsgGA/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPRwX-tW8VI/AAAAAAAABIc/lepwVpxsgGA/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\nvirtual teaming is not a tennis match where ideas are lobbed to and fro on email between a few dominant personalities sitting in shore office , ill equipped for the task with everybody else looks on helplessly. reflection time soothes the effect of upsetting voice mail or email if on line etiquette is not fully followed . the team leaders task is to release and harness the potential latent in the virtual team. He does not suppress conflict rather he channels it. He must not abdicate or take sides \u2013rather he remains the impartial arbitrator. He has the maturity to invite team members of the relevant expertise to kickstart change\u2014and wont feel threatened .<br />\n<br />\nHe wears his authority lightly and he reduces his role to a minimum. <br />\nTao te ching spake 2000 years back\u2014<br />\nThe best conqueror does not take part in the war<br />\nThe best employer of men keeps himself below them<br />\nThis is the called the ability of using men\u2014<br />\n--and women<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a advocating vehemently what they believe is right. however leader ship and respect for authority remain in place\u2014the dynamic thing is the freedom in decision making for the team members depending on their own areas of expertise. <br />\n<br />\nso here is an oath for the virtual team:<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a be vulnerable and change personal traits to manage this change. i agree to shift from the role model reinforced rigid mindset to a flexible future focused mindset. i recognise that the rules of the game has changed and that even as a leader of change i am on a learning curve. i commit myself to transparent and clear communications for 360 degrees feedback<br />\n<br />\nsome thoughts on pitfalls of real teaming meetings under the single roof<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: bring people together to sound them <br />\n<br />\na group can think only as well as its most proficient member on the topic \u2013the tongue must taste and the ear must hear \u2013 not vice versa --right?<br />\n<br />\nwhen meetings succeed it can be felt and when it fails it can be felt even better<br />\n<br />\na failed meeting can do a lot of harm <br />\n<br />\nquite often solving a problem just needs the attention of just one single expert rather than the time and wasted energies of a whole onlooking gaping bunch<br />\n<br />\nsome team sub managers use a meeting to buffer them from frightening decisions\u2014 safety in numbers<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a challenge <br />\n<br />\na dictatorial topgun chair can repress discussion rather than control it <br />\n<br />\nif the chair can hold the interest the comfort of the venue is not important<br />\n<br />\na meetings success is judged from the actions that it forced <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nOur much misunderstood ulysses software is basically an open , written and thus permanent ( not a passing fad ) employee suggestion system which cuts across departmental lines and rank levels. it allows \u201cstructured upwards and down wards communications\u201d under one roof or different. virtual teaming to grass root levels is possible under the same roof or different roofs using this as one of the tools. <br />\n<br />\nimagine a ulyssess program for upward and down ward communications being filled up by the manchester united soccer team after every match\u2014the idea being to foster openness and transparency among team members ---with sensitivity and caring, of course. <br />\n<br />\nfrom manager to goalkeeper/ <em>stop looking at the girls and signing autographs when a match is going on.</em><br />\n<br />\nfrom captain to center forward/ <em>concentrate on not being offside when the corner kick is taken.</em><br />\n<br />\nfrom coach to star striker / <em>to confuse and shake off the guy tagging you cheek by jowl once every 15 minutes interchange positions with the midfielder briefly for 2 minutes.</em><br />\n<em><br />\n</em><br />\netc etc <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a feedback without getting defensive\u2014and the team can watch who is falling into the same hole again and again and letting the whole adventure down. the culture of not retaliating for people telling the truth as they see it from their perspective now develops. people are introduced to the culture that they must be open to perceptions others have on their performance even if they do not agree. and there must be a follow up to those who provide the feedback. maturity lies in not getting defensive and punishing others for being honest with you.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; or to provide status updates. action items can be clearly stated. the prose must be thoughtful and meaningful as it is permanent. ideas can be channelled to the appropriate expert for evaluation. this results of which can be can be communicated back in a timely manner. this basket software facilitates the team members to utilise their creative and analytical ideas ( and still retain the patent \u2013 i will talk of office politics as a DC later ).<br />\n<br />\nulysses realises that the most successful organisations , especially in the chemical field, are learning machines who keep harvesting ideas. it recognises that every sailor is capable of generating improvement ideas and that a formal system is required to manage ideas. the grassroot level is more familiar with daily problems and inefficiencies / frustrations of their jobs especially when the management is an unseen outdated non english speaking monarch who is only interested in filing dishonest reports not actual facts. <br />\n<br />\nwhat was good 20 years back may be unacceptable in this modern age. ulysses works on the principle that every thing can be improved. some team members can bring the best practises from previous employers. a rewarding experience with one suggestion can lead to another one for the system will not allow personality problems to affect decisions. ulysses sets rest to fears that ideas may be ignored , ridiculed or stolen or even blocked by opponents. most humans when they hear an idea they know will gain them recognition will pass it off as their own. <br />\n<br />\nulysses realises that the race for quality has no finish line. it ensures that questions and concerns have to be analysed and responded to within a time frame. for quick response time is the most important element of a successful suggestion programme. when used well to benefit the company and its employees it is a morale booster.<br />\n<br />\nof course this must have an off limits agenda and framework. it cannot be used as a collective bargaining tool ( likewhat happens at TESMA seminars ) or to wrangle more overtime \u2013unless it is solution oriented, has a better / less tiring method , reduces paperwork or challenges old obsolete habits.<br />\n<br />\nthe software can be further developed to include a tracking module for date recd, date closed, adopted/ not adopted/ under consideration/ unfeasible due to budget constraints. <br />\n<br />\nonce ulysses takes off it will debunk the 80/20 rule\u2014that 80% of the best suggestions come from 20% of the population. all my ex chief officers ajay/ amit/ sanjay/ pankaj/ jain / rahul/ prasad all will vouch that is comes to 90/95 for this\u2014as i hold a oral ulysses exercise on the bridge every month. and remember any thing you do must be measured, lest you lose control. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a suggest the training to fill up the gaps and thus convert the weaker areas into strengths. it can be used to reverse negative trends to develop specific action plans for moulding individual behaviours that can improve team performance. best practises learnt from other companies can be communicated sideways or upwards.<br />\n<br />\nmultipoint feedback is an effective and ideal tool into motivating
