Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "28", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8193875144415239426/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "2444447971250096521", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-11-27T00:26:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-14T14:56:46+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkyMzE4ODA2NDYyCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/11/sampling-procedures-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2444447971250096521", "title": "SAMPLING PROCEDURES CHEMICAL TANKERS -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br />\n&nbsp;&nbsp; SAMPLING PROCEDURES -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPABt0UY8cI/AAAAAAAAA04/NbClEVvEgnQ/s1600/imagesCA42O685.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPABt0UY8cI/AAAAAAAAA04/NbClEVvEgnQ/s1600/imagesCA42O685.jpg\" /></a></div>Chemical cargo samples are evidence of the condition of the product during various phases like loading, passage, discharging . <br />\n<br />\nSampling is done to protect against cargo claims especially when barges are involved.&nbsp; How many samples are taken depends on the type of cargo. <br />\n<br />\nSamples will normally be drawn prior to loading and upon completion. Similarly, at the discharge port, prior to discharge. Shore tank samples are not witnessed by ship staff , and is done by an approved surveyor.<br />\n<br />\nAt the start of the transfer one sample to be taken at the ships manifold on shore side <span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">with the ships manifold valve SHUT in a clear glass bottle, </span>visually checked and retained. The Chief officer or the duty officer must witness this important sample. If the sample is milky or obvious foreign matter is present , then take another sample .The valve to the tank should be opened up only if the manifold&nbsp; sample is acceptable. <br />\n<br />\nSo it is important to know the type of pump used ashore for pumping. If a screw / gear pump or reciprocating pump is used the cargo hose will rupture. Centrifugal pump will not cause any such problems. <br />\n<br />\nCompressed air used for line blowing must be dry. Shore line is usually pigged. The pig must be inspected if feasible and checked to be&nbsp; free of moisture , odour or cargo residues.<br />\n<br />\nOn the sample bottle label the ships name, voyage number, date, location, type of sample (manifold, tank etc ), product name. Retention period is one year. Prior to disposal take permission from operator. <br />\n<br />\nCargo and Fuel samples are not to brought into the accommodation.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nThe vessel is to keep a full set of samples for owners benefit, these are to be retained on board in sealed and marked bottles for a period of 12 months after completion of dischg, after which they can be disposed in a proper manner. Reactive samples must not be placed together<br />\n<br />\nBefore discharge, samples are to be taken from the ship\u2019s side of the valve with the manifold valve closed.&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nIn some terminals, depending on the product, the vessel may be requested to load \u201cfoot samples\u201d. Foot sample consist of a small amount of the product being loaded to a depth sufficient to enable the cargo surveyor to take a complete representative sample from the ship\u2019s tanks. These samples will then be delivered to the laboratory ashore for quality testing regarding contamination. When loading foot samples, ensure the loading rate is suitable as regards loading only the minimum quantity requested by the surveyor. The ullage/sounding must be constantly monitored to ensure that excessive product is not loaded. <br />\n<br />\nThese samples will then be delivered to the laboratory ashore for quality testing wrt contamination. When loading foot samples, ensure the loading rate is suitable. Also load only the minimum quantity required by the surveyor. The ullage must be constantly monitored to ensure that excessive product is not loaded. If first foot samples are taken a log entry should be made.<br />\n<br />\nIf there is an alleged claim for contaminated cargo the Master must: -<br />\n<br />\nImmediately call in the local representative of the vessel\u2019s P&amp;I club.<br />\nNotify Operator about the alleged claim and confirm that the P&amp;I representative is attending.<br />\nTake good care of vessel\u2019s sealed cargo samples, i.e.<br />\nbefore loading sample<br />\nfirst foot sample<br />\nbefore discharge sample<br />\n&nbsp;--and not hand them to anyone, except in agreement with the P&amp;I representative, and only against written receipt.<br />\nAssist the P&amp;I representative in connection with the relevant (joint) surveys and analysis.<br />\nSign no document related to the alleged contamination other than after consultation with the P&amp;I representative.<br />\n<br />\n<em>Recapitualtion:</em><br />\n<br />\nSampling at--<br />\n<br />\n<strong>Loadport:</strong>Manifold foot sample with manifold valve shut<br />\nFirst foot inside tank if applicable<br />\nTank samples at completion of loading.<br />\nIn case the manifold composite sample is no good take the initial contents into one tank only and record it in the remarks column of SOF.<br />\n<br />\n<strong>Disport:</strong>Sample of each tank.<br />\nManifold sample at start of discharging<br />\nSample bottle lable must have the date , name and signature of chief officer and surveyor<br />\nSampling is a risky process. When taking samples from pipeline drain cocks ensure the line is depressurized.&nbsp; The person must wear proper PPE as justified after reading the MSDS sheets.<br />\nUTI samplers can be used to do closed sampling as long as the extension tube is peforated along the entire length. <br />\n<br />\nOn ships with nitrogen plant this UTI tube extension ( for 30 minute static dissipation time saving ) has no value and packs huge nuisance potential, IF&nbsp; it is only perforated at the top , and not along entire length. <br />\n<br />\na)high mp cargoes will freeze inside and will restrict sampler from going down by gravity. <br />\n<br />\nb)source of contamination. <br />\n<br />\nc)ullage for foaming cargoes like veh=g oils/ molasses is not representative of tank content. <br />\n<br />\nd)temperature of UTI is not representative of tank content. <br />\n<br />\ne)with sediment cargoes UTI ullage is not accurate. <br />\n<br />\nf) first foot sample failure can occur due to no fault of ship. <br />\n<br />\ng) the wedge formula used for calculating yard provided ullage tables becomes redundant \u2013as the formula is based on tape assuming vertical position by gravity. <br />\n<br />\nh)certain cargoes like latex can never be loaded , though possible to load by COF and SS resistance tables. <br />\n<br />\ni) few litres of heavier water at tank bottom will be pushed up into non perforated extension pipe by lighter inmixible cargo on top \u2013and UTI readings will indicate full tank of water while the cargo tank actually has negligible water. Wrong bill of lading figures can cause financial disaster.<br />\n<br />\nj) The slop tank water interface will not be accurate on annex 1 ships, and entries in oil record book will be wrong wrt oil and water interface quantities.<br />\n<br />\nSample bottles must be properly stowed in a dedicated sample locker. Samples must never ever be brought into the CCR or accommodation living space. The sample locker racks and cell divisions must be fully resistant to the chemical cargoes intended to be stowed. If a bottle breaks inside the sample locker it must still be contained by a SS tray, and should not seep out on deck. The locker should have high and low vents for high and low VD gases. There must be 2 lockers so that incompatible bottles are stowed together. Samples must be in glass bottles and not polythene bottles.<br />\n<br />\nCertain chemicals like propylene oxide and acrylic acid samples are disposed off as soon as the cargo is discharged without claims , due to their hazardous nature.<br />\n<br />\nDEFINITIONS:<br />\n<br />\nAll-levels sample: A sample obtained by submerging a stoppered beaker or bottle to a point as near as possible to the draw-off level, then opening the sampler and raising it at a rate such that it is<br />\napproximately three-fourths full as it emerges from the liquid. An all-levels sample is not necessarily a<br />\nrepresentative sample because the tank volume may not be proportional to the depth and because the operator may not be able to raise the sampler at the variable rate required for proportional filling. The rate of filling is proportional to the square root of the depth of immersion<br />\n<br />\nBottom sample: spot sample taken from the product at or close to the bottom of a tank or container.<br />\n<br />\nClearance sample: spot sample taken at a specified distance below the bottom of the tank outlet. Composite sample (weighted): sample obtained by combining a number of spot samples in defined proportions so as to obtain a sample representative of the bulk of the product<br />\n<br />\nDead bottom sample: spot sample taken from a point on the tank bottom. Note: Such samples require the use of a device with a bottom opening, commonly used for free water samples.<br />\n<br />\nDrain sample: sample obtained from the water draw-off point on a storage tank.<br />\n\u2018first foot\u2019 sample: sample drawn from a vessel tank early during a cargo loading, when the depth of product in the tank(s) is approximately 300 mm, (one foot).<br />\n<br />\nNote: Regulations concerning the dissipation of static charge normally require the cessation of pumping and a relaxation time of thirty minutes before \u2018first foot\u2019 samples are drawn.<br />\nLower sample: spot sample taken at a level of five-sixths of the depth of liquid below the top surface Middle sample: spot sample taken at a level of one-half of the depth of liquid below the top surface Multi-tank composite sample: a mixture of individual samples or composites of samples that have<br />\nbeen obtained from several tanks or ship/barge compartments containing the same grade of material<br />\n<br />\nRunning sample: sample obtained with an apparatus which accumulates the sample while passing in both directions through the total liquid height, excluding any free water.Note: The apparatus passes through the liquid at such a rate that it is approximately 80% full as it emerges from the liquid.<br />\n<br />\nSingle tank composite sample: blend prepared from the upper, middle and lower samples from a single tank<br />\n<br />\nSkim sample (surface sample): spot sample taken from the surface of the liquid.<br />\n<br />\nSpot sample: sample taken at a specific location in a tank or from a pipeline.<br />\n<br />\nSuction level sample (outlet sample): sample taken at the lowest level from which liquid hydrocarbon is pumped from the tank.<br />\n<br />\nTap sample: A spot sample taken via a tap, typically located on the side of the shore tank.<br />\n<br />\nTop sample: spot sample obtained 150 mm (6\u201d) below the top surface of the liquid<br />\n<br />\nUpper sample: spot sample taken at a level of one-sixth of the depth of liquid below the top surface<br />\n<br />\nZone sample (core sample, flow through sample): sample taken as that part of the liquid column which is contained within the whole height of the sampler when it is sealed at a single spot location within a tank.--<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc4UAWTSLI/AAAAAAAAB4E/pcht9tMfqSg/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc4UAWTSLI/AAAAAAAAB4E/pcht9tMfqSg/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<br />\n..", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "6", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2444447971250096521/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "2507917714325871558", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-11-26T23:46:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-09-24T10:12:18+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzE2ODM5MzM4Nzc3Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/11/methanol-spray-on-chemical-tankers-capt.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2507917714325871558", "title": "METHANOL SPRAY ON CHEMICAL TANKERS--  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_3rofiiyI/AAAAAAAAA0o/AT1xli2Z9JI/s1600/graco.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_3rofiiyI/AAAAAAAAA0o/AT1xli2Z9JI/s1600/graco.jpg\" /></a></div>METHANOL SPRAY IS THE BIGGEST BULLSHIT GOIN' ON AT SEA--<br />\n<br />\nso--what are you doing?&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nyou just spray methanol where ever the surveyor who will do wallwash, &nbsp;can physically reach!&nbsp;&nbsp; -- as he is NOT a bird--<br />\n<br />\nso you have pre-empted the medium in his squirt bottle. All the muck is brought down to the bottom. The wall wash of the tank bottom is usually never done.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nbut all this extra smartness can undo you-- if you fail the first foot.<br />\n<br />\nit is better to fail the wall wash than the first foot.<br />\n<br />\n#######<br />\n<br />\nA Chemical tanker sailor at sea must care for his OWN safety. <br />\n<br />\nHis ignorant Captain and rogue Shipmanagement Company , will force him to spray Methanol using SCBA sets . <br />\n<br />\nRemember, SCBA is for rescue from enclosed spaces, after an Emergency Alarm of 7 short one long blast-- -- NOT routine work inside cargo tanks ( like Methanol spray ). <br />\n<br />\nIn the IBC code , \" working time \" has been erroneously read by vested interests as official sanction to do routine WORK inside chemical cargo tanks. <br />\n<br />\nIT IS NOT SO. <br />\n<br />\n\" WORKING TIME \" IS TO BE READ AS \" LUNG DEMAND TIME \" <br />\n<br />\n-- WHICH IS 100 LITRES OF FREE AIR A MINUTE FOR STRAIN ( OF FIREMANS LIFT RESCUE) , 30 LITRES A MINUTE FOR LIGHT ACTIVITY , AND 10 LITRES A MINUTE WHILE AT REST.<br />\n<br />\n#############<br />\n<br />\nGUIDELINES FOR METHANOL SPRAY<br />\n<br />\nFirst of all secure all ingnition sources --as the fumes can travel.&nbsp; Many chemical tankers had explosions while Methanol spray-- the bodies were NEVER found in one piece.<br />\n<br />\nMethanol is NOT a static accumulator, like Toluene.&nbsp; Toluene must NEVER EVER be sprayed!<br />\n<br />\nMethanol spray requires a Risk Assessment form to be filled in conjunction with a Enclosed spaces entry form--and signed. &nbsp;Do it on the Matrix of SEVERITY&nbsp; to PERIOD OF IMPACT/ CERTAINTY.&nbsp; or this RA is not worth the paper it is made on.<br />\n<br />\nRead the Methanol MSDS sheet.<br />\n<br />\nEducate the work crew about the dangers .<br />\n<br />\nMethanol is a non static generator and you can use a barrel pump at good pressure if required.<br />\n<br />\nThe workforce must be proficient in wearing AIRLINE sets-- here the pressures are monitored from outside tank.<br />\n<br />\nMethanol spray must be done only in daylight hours as far as practicable.<br />\n<br />\nThe sprayer must wear full chemical resistant gas suit not oilskins.<br />\n<br />\nOutside the tank SCBA set and harness/ line must be available for rescue .<br />\n<br />\nMethanol should be sprayed only after the entire cleaning operation is over as the final polish up act\u2014or the whole thing is wasted.<br />\n<br />\nTest the methanol drum for chlorides. UCC wants 0.249 PPM chlorides for MEG FG .<br />\n<br />\nRun a PTT test on the drum methanol and check if it holds at least one hour.<br />\n<br />\nUsually Methanol spray is done with a dedicated barrel pump. <br />\n<br />\nFlush the pump and hose with DI water before and after use.<br />\n<br />\nInitial Methanol spray-- waste it into the sump to flush out line contents.<br />\n<br />\nMethanol will extract chlorides, HC , and colour if it came from steam ( not from previous cargoes ) from the bulkhead.<br />\n<br />\nIf chlorides are your only problem use DI water.<br />\n<br />\nPrior to spraying place a M2 wilden pump in tank impeller sump to eject it from the tank. This will reduce the gas freeing time and reduce the methanol mist inside the tank.<br />\n<br />\nGive 2 runs. <br />\n<br />\nIt is best done by one sprayer following the other. <br />\n<br />\nThe leading dirty edge must be washed to the bottom . If it dries up half way on the bulkead it can be seen visually.<br />\n<br />\nSpray from ford to aft and top to bottom.&nbsp; use a wilden pump at the sump , to pump out methanol --to reduce the gas in the tank.<br />\n<br />\nGas feeing after the job is best done while running steam coils.<br />\n<br />\nThe muck brought down to the bottom must be removed with sponges and DI water.<br />\n<br />\nCheck the gas content using Draeger tubes. Bring it down to 50% of TLV.<br />\n<br />\nDo wall wash .<br />\n<br />\n#########<br />\n<br />\nGenerally sonsidered as a universal solvent, because it is aggressive towards HC and substances not soluble in water, being completely soluble in water itself. Methanol is intoxicating but not directly poisonous.<br />\n<br />\nColourless <br />\nWatery liquid<br />\nAlcohol odour when pure<br />\nFlammable<br />\nToxic vapors at room temp.<br />\nIngestion/ ihalation poisoning can cause dizziness, unconsciousness , blindness ( if drunk ) and sighing respiration<br />\nCheck for chlorides when you receive the drums. Must have cert for PTT&gt; 60 min<br />\nNon static generator<br />\nCat Y<br />\nUSCG/ 20<br />\nVP 92 mm hg at 20C<br />\nBP/ 64C<br />\nFP/ 12C<br />\nVD/ 1.1<br />\nCompletely soluble in water\u2014due to ionic bonding<br />\nSteaming\u20149 litres on 100 cum to ensure LEL is not exceeded<br />\nTLV 200 ppm<br />\nAIT/ 464C<br />\nST/ 22.6 dynes / cm at 20C<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nRemarks: <br />\nMethanol shelf life must be monitored\u2014test the methanol before use\u2014lest it fails a clean tank.<br />\n<br />\nIt is the simplest alcohol, and is a light, volatile, colourless, flammable, poisonous liquid with a distinctive odor . <br />\n<br />\nA Methanol flame is almost colorless. Methanol is intoxicating but not directly poisonous. It is toxic by its breakdown (toxication) by the enzyme Alcohol Dehydrogenase in the liver by forming Formic acid and Formaldehyde which cause blindness by destruction of the optic nerve. <br />\n<br />\nThough it is miscible with water, Methanol is very hard to wash off the skin; it is best to treat Methanol like gasoline. <br />\n<br />\nThe initial symptoms of Methanol intoxication are those of central nervous system depression: headache, dizziness, nausea, lack of coordination, confusion, drowsiness, and with suffiently large doses, unconsciousness and death. Once the initial symptoms have passed, a second set of symptoms arises 10\u201330 hours after the initial exposure to Methanol: blurring or complete loss of vision, together with acidosis. These symptoms result from the accumulation of toxic levels of Formate in the bloodstream, and may progress to death by respiratory failure. <br />\n<br />\nEthanol is sometimes denatured (adulterated), and thus made undrinkable, by the addition of methanol. The result is known as methylated spirit. <br />\n<br />\nUnlike petroleum fires, Methanol fires can be extinguished with plain water (while Methanol is less dense than water, they are miscible, and the addition of water will cause the fire to use its heat to boil the water).<br />\n<br />\nREMEMBER- METHANOL CANNOT DISSOLVE SALT.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ec5hhZyywaE/Tn1fmdSit3I/AAAAAAAAGcs/Lv_AQNkNl4k/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil+2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ec5hhZyywaE/Tn1fmdSit3I/AAAAAAAAGcs/Lv_AQNkNl4k/s320/capt+ajit+vadakayil+2.JPG\" width=\"199\" /></a></div><br />\n-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 29 years in command )</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "2", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2507917714325871558/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "7030391948297594663", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-11-26T23:30:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-11-26T23:30:57+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkwNzk0NDU3NTYwCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/11/ph-chemical-tankers-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7030391948297594663", "title": "pH , CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1SlGDOeI/AAAAAAAAA0c/4LXYM8xHLQI/s1600/imagesCA79PJ08.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1SlGDOeI/AAAAAAAAA0c/4LXYM8xHLQI/s1600/imagesCA79PJ08.jpg\" /></a></div>pH CHEMICAL TANKERS --CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\nA chemical parcel man must understand the pH scale. <br />\n<br />\nFor example--- Zinc tanks can take cargoes only between pH 6 to 9 or zinc will shed and contaminate the cargo. Most epoxies cannot take pH less than 3.5, though the manufacturer will NEVER declare this.<br />\n<br />\nThe pH scale is from zero to 14.<br />\n<br />\nNeutral fresh water pH is zero . In pure water which is neutral, the conc of Hydrogen ion is 10 raised to -7 equivalent/litre which corresponds to pH of 7. <br />\n<br />\nZero pH is an acid of highest strength like Hydrochloric acid . pH 14 is a base of highest strength like Caustic .<br />\n<br />\npH is a measure of hydrogen ion concentration in that solution. A small change in pH represents a large change in hydrogen ion concentration<span style=\"color: yellow;\">.</span><span style=\"background-color: red;\"><em><span style=\"color: yellow;\"> As the conc of H+ ions increase by 10 times, the value of pH decreases by one unit and vice versa</span>.</em></span> This is because the pH scale is logarithmic. This means each change of one in pH value is 10 times more acidic. <br />\n<br />\nSo a substance with pH 2 is 1000 times more acidic than one with pH 5. In other words ( better to understand this well ) diluting a strong acid of pH 2 , ten times increase the pH value to pH 3.<br />\n<br />\nAcidic soil is infertile, so lime is added. Thiobacillus ferro oxidans ( bacteria ) lowers pH to 2 or even 0.7. Some lakes are fairly acidic ( pH 3.7 to 5.5 ). Be aware when a charterer while trying to save some money for TCFW tells you to dilute say molasses cargo with lake intake. Boiler feed water water cannot be acidic so additives are added to keep it basic. <br />\n<br />\nNeutral or pure water has an equal conc of H+ ions and OH- ions. When an acid is added the conc of H+ ions become greater than that of OH- ions. Similarly when a base is added the conc of OH- ions increases while that of H+ decreases. <br />\n<br />\nThus an acid solution is one in which H+ is greater than 10 raised to -7.<br />\n<br />\npH changes with temp. It decreases on heating. pH of boiling water is 6.56.<br />\n<br />\nThe pH of DI water drops from 7 to 5.5 due to some reaction in water when splashed in air. Rain ph is 5.6 as CO2 dissolves to form carbonic acid. This is the reason why the DI water spray turns slightly acidic<br />\n<br />\nFew pH values:---<br />\n<br />\nHydrochloric acid/ 0<br />\nGastric stomach juice/ 1<br />\nCoca cola/ 2.5<br />\nOrange juice /3.0<br />\nTomato/ 4.1<br />\nBlack coffee/5<br />\nUrine/ 6<br />\nMilk/ 6.6<br />\nFresh water/ 7<br />\nBlood/ 7.4<br />\nSea water/ 8<br />\nTooth paste/ 9.9<br />\nAmmonia/ 11.9<br />\nCaustic/ 14<br />\n<br />\nPrior loading certain cargoes the pH value of the tank internals and attachments are taken to make sure they are neutral ( Phenol ).<br />\n<br />\nCanned food is sterilized by lowering pH using acidulants like citric, acetic, fumaric, ascorbic, propionic, lactic, adipic, tartaric etc.<br />\n<br />\npH in water at room temp 25C-- there is only one hydrogen ion for every 555 million water molecules. Basically ph scale measures the amount of H+ and OH-. <br />\n<br />\nA person cannot survive if his blood ph drops to 7 or rises to 7.8. The buffering capacity of blood prevents such swings in pH level. <br />\n<br />\nThe gentleman who invented pH wanted to know how acidic his beer was. Beer needs yeast and yeast uses enzymes. Enzymes work only if pH is right. Beer is pH3<br />\n<br />\nFor the erudite\u2014 The pH of a solution depends on the concentration of ionized protons and not the total concentration of acid. If there is an excess of protons it is an acidic solution. If there is a shortage of protons it is basic. <br />\n<br />\nBufferclean 5.5 removes all zinc white salts and brings it down like snow fall. <br />\n<br />\nBuffer solution resists any change of its pH value due to dilution or an addition of solution of acid/ alkali. The process by which H+ or OH- ions are removed so that pH remains constant is known as buffer action.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1YuEMVyI/AAAAAAAAA0g/KIL1C4jqybo/s1600/imagesCA7O9SVE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1YuEMVyI/AAAAAAAAA0g/KIL1C4jqybo/s1600/imagesCA7O9SVE.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1db3GdSI/AAAAAAAAA0k/CSYU7ob9iNc/s1600/imagesCA0C8YNY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO_1db3GdSI/AAAAAAAAA0k/CSYU7ob9iNc/s1600/imagesCA0C8YNY.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<br />\n..", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "1", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7030391948297594663/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4580975739258452054", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-11-26T11:18:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-11-26T21:10:51+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkwNzg2MDUxOTgxCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/11/block-and-bleed-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4580975739258452054", "title": "BLOCK AND BLEED ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></b><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 16pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">BLOCK AND BLEED ARRANGEMENT </span></b><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">( IN LIEU OF DECK SEAL )</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9HBFv6-HI/AAAAAAAAAyM/lxP4gyfRZfE/s1600/imagesCANYK7ZF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9HBFv6-HI/AAAAAAAAAyM/lxP4gyfRZfE/s1600/imagesCANYK7ZF.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9HGi_bdVI/AAAAAAAAAyQ/kcG9-6S9qjs/s1600/untitled.bmp\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9HGi_bdVI/AAAAAAAAAyQ/kcG9-6S9qjs/s1600/untitled.bmp\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9Jz2EFP8I/AAAAAAAAAyY/7_S0J_vl_eI/s1600/imagesCA37KD8J.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO9Jz2EFP8I/AAAAAAAAAyY/7_S0J_vl_eI/s1600/imagesCA37KD8J.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">ON CHEMICAL TANKERS WHICH CARRY WATER SENSITIVE ( LIKE MEG FG ) &nbsp;AND WATER AGGRESSIVE CARGOES ( SULPHURIC ACID )--&nbsp; IT IS OBVIOUS THAT SHIP CANNOT HAVE A DECK SEAL WITH WATER MEDIUM.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If cargo vapours enter the nitrogen membrane system/ CMS system -- the plant can be kissed goodbye!</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hence Nitrogen plants piping system will have a Block and Bleed arrangement.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Company policy requires that the Block and Bleed valves, be require properly<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>maintenaned at regular intervals and all the valves (Regulating valve, Block valves, Bleed valve, Non-Return valve and the Deck Main Isolating valve) be regularly tested for proper operation and tightness. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Unlike the fool proof deck seal, this arrangement requires close monitoring and testing alarms for safety.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When chemical tankers with a Nitrogen plant carries both chemical and Annex 1 cargoes, a BLOCK AND BLEED arrangement is used instead of a deck seal, to prevent backflow from cargo tank into IG plant and safe non-cargo spaces.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is an<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\"> arrangement consisting of two shut-off block valves in series with a venting to atmosphere bleed valve in between (double block and bleed).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>It is between the DMV and the GRV . The operation of the valves is to be automatically executed. Signals for opening/ closing is to be taken from the process </span></span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">directly, e.g. inert gas flow or differential pressure.</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: italic;\">Alarm for faulty operation of the valves is to be provided, e.g. the operation status of \u201cBlower Stop\u201d and \u201csupply valves open\u201d is an alarm condition\u201d.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The size of the bleed valve should be such that it will not allow pressure build-up from back-flow of hydrocarbons in the event that the block and bleed arrangement and the non return valve) fail to achieve their function. Block and Bleed arrangement is triggered by zero flow condition. The differential pressure arrangement will sense the difference between the pressure in the line upstream of the pressure regulating valve and the pressure in the IG main.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If the pressure in the IG main is higher than the pressure upstream of the control valve, the system will close the gas regulating valve and shut down automatically. Indication of this condition should be provided in the Engine Control Room and the Cargo Control Room. The measuring points should be arranged to preclude bypass of hydrocarbons from the tanks into the engine room via the sensing lines by, for example, using secondary 3 to 15 p.s.i. loop signal in lieu of direct signal or by using other suitable electronic sensors. A timing mechanism, providing a few seconds delay, should be included into the starting sequence to permit the blower to start while the pressure in the tanks is higher than the pressure at the blower discharge. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The effectiveness of the Block and Bleed devices depends on their ability to sense the \u201cprocess\u201d fluid (Inert Gas) pressure or flow. In some instances, deficient systems have been built with Block and Bleed arrangements which do not sense the \u201cprocess\u201d fluid but rely on the blower operational \u201con\u201d / \u201coff\u201d status to operate the Block and Bleed valves and achieve the sealing function. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">For Block and Bleed arrangements which do not have differential pressure or flow sensing devices, it is possible that, during periods of cargo discharge operation with the blower operational, the tank pressure may increase to a point higher than the inert gas generator discharge pressure.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In this case, cargo gases back-flow into the machinery space could occur if the Non-Return valve was defective. Thus, when the Block and Bleed arrangements depend on the blower \u201con\u201d / \u201coff\u201d condition, there is effectively only one protective non-return device in the system, namely the Non-Return valve. Such arrangement does not conform as an alternative arrangement providing a measure of safety \u201c<b>Equivalent</b>\u201d to that of a water seal.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The minimum hardware recommended for proper Block and Bleed arrangement are indicated below. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">1. Block and Bleed control to be based on signals from a differential pressure or flow sensing detector of the \u201cprocess\u201d fluid, Inert Gas or Nitrogen.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">2. Provision of an audible and visual alarm for low differential pressure or low flow if the block valves remain open.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">3. Provision of an audible and visual alarm for faulty operation of the block and bleed valves. Blower \u201cstop\u201d and supply valves \u201copen\u201d should be an alarm condition.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">4. Audible and visual alarm to be provided if valve position is mismatched ((i.e. if Block Valves and Bleed Valve are closed) \u2013 this function to be provided with a time delay.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">5. Provision of indication in the Cargo Control room of \u201copen\u201d and \u201cclosed\u201d status of the block and bleed valves, the Gas Regulating valve, and Bleed to Atmosphere valve.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">6. Provision of control air for the Block and Bleed Valves to be via an independent solenoid valve arrangement from the solenoid supplying the Regulating Valve (Bulkhead Valve).</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">7. The pressure sensors used for the block and bleed control should be independent from the pressure sensor required by SOLAS Regulation 62.16.1.1 (equivalent Regulation 14.1.1 on Reference A)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">8. Provision of interlock to ensure that Blower shutdown will close the Block and Bleed arrangement and that the Block and Bleed arrangement cannot be opened unless blower power is on. Also, the blower should be arranged so that it cannot start unless the block valves are closed.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The bleed ( vent ) to atmosphere is best operated by power.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Flow diagram schematics:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">N2 plant\u2014 valve-- -vent to atmosphere--- pressure transmitter--- GRV/ safe area to dangerous area/ bleed to atmosphere with flame screen ---<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; &nbsp;</span>block and bleed arrangement ( in lieu of deck seal )--- NR valve\u2014 pressure transmitter of differential pressure device.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;, &quot;sans-serif&quot;; ( maximum student suicides on the planet is from this dept at Cornell )<br />\n<br />\nhis partner for the project is a&nbsp;South Korean boy&nbsp;.<br />\n<br />\nany moving HUMAN BEING is pinged&nbsp; . <br />\n<br />\nthe program&nbsp;detects only human forms.<br />\n<br />\nin this video my son tried to slip though the college atrium at night -- but the camera pings him and then will track him , no matter what he tries--<br />\n<br />\nIn the background, a car moves and its reflection comes on the glass pane of the hall -- the program pings the driver of the car in a split second-- and then you can zoom in--<br />\n<br />\nwho says a human eye ( with persistance of vision ) can match a computer eye , when it comes to security?<br />\n<br />\nthe old professor proudly calls these two blokes-- &nbsp;his A TEAM!<br />\n<br />\nThis project got the 2nd prize ( students vote ) at Cornell, --they lost by one single vote . />\n<br />\nthis is a true story--<br />\n<br />\nwhen ole capt vadakayil was mistaken for a anaconda snake charmer --<br />\n<br />\nwe went to rostock with iron ore loaded by conveyor belt from paradip --<br />\n<br />\n6 hours before arrival , i got all 5 holds opened out --<br />\n<br />\nchief officer came to me and said -- sir, someone is playing mischief-- a black hawser is lying on top of the ore in hold no 3 --<br />\n<br />\ni interjected-- but, all our dang&nbsp;hawsers are yellow!<br />\n<br />\ni went on deck-- threw a steel nut on the coiled mass --<br />\n<br />\n--- a HUGE python slithered --<br />\n<br />\nimmediately 60 gaping crew assembled to see this terrific sight-- i drove the duty engineer away , for, in the excitement the engine room was abandoned --<br />\n<br />\n3 young cadets nearly fainted , as just 2 days after paradip they went insideall holds to check for daylight ( battening down and checking packing integrity )- -<br />\n<br />\nwe garrotted the python using extreme seamanship -- and got it on maindeck -- we smashed the poor guys head to pulp--<br />\n<br />\nsomeone suggested-- let us throw the dang thing overboard--<br />\n<br />\nsomeone else said -- no&nbsp;, violation of marpol regulation annex 5 , section so and so , blah blah--<br />\n<br />\nso it finally transpired, &nbsp;that it was taken to engine room in a huge sack by 4 huffin' and&nbsp;puffin' sailors -- taking turns-- <br />\n<br />\nwe decided to incinerate it hush hush , while discharging ore -- to avoid a possible quarantine problem<br />\n<br />\nas soon as we berthed 3 bristling and restless german shepherd dogs came along with communist customs-- <br />\n<br />\n--they went crazy -- sniff sniff-- strange new smell --<br />\n<br />\ncustoms got panicky -- dogs ran down to engine room-- started sniffing , pawing and barking at the huge sack -- placed next to incinerator--<br />\n<br />\ncustoms cried -- AAAHAA -- at least 60 kilos of 'm drugs! -- <br />\n<br />\nwow! we have struck pay dirt --<br />\n<br />\nthey opened up the sack in triumph--<br />\n<br />\nthe snake stirred despite a missing head -- bizzare!<br />\n<br />\nall screamed and ran helter skelter, &nbsp;like the whirling dervishes --<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;one white faced sweinstieger type customs guy was caught in&nbsp;dead end funnel deck ladder --<br />\n<br />\ndogs broke their leashes and ran pell mell , down gangway on to jetty --<br />\n<br />\n--uncontrollable --<br />\n<br />\n5 red faced german mannschaft customs officers come running in to mE cabin--<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;\" CAPTAIN ,&nbsp;PLEEASE FOR OUR OWN SAFETY -- HOW MANY MORE SNAKES YOU HAVE ON SHIP?\"<br />\n<br />\ni said laconically -- \" as far as i know, only one-- and it is dead! \" --<br />\n<br />\nthey were still darting glances fearfully into my bedroom -- till they left-- probably for that turban and&nbsp; flute, which they get to see on tv<br />\n<br />\nlater pretty rostock zoo ladies came runnin' to see the dead reptile -- and cried -- \" you should have donated this lovely creature to the zoo!\" --<br />\n<br />\nwe incinerated the poor guy -- (or was it a gal? ) -- -- after cutting it into pieces, with a circular saw -- 6 consignments into the furnace =<br />\n<br />\n--&nbsp;despite eating nothing for a month inside the hold --- it was full of beef--<br />\n<br />\nwe did the incineration job for 2 days -- the whole engine room smelled of TANDOORI chicken!<br />\n<br />\nwell-- this was before the berlin wall came down -<br />\n<br />\nnow-- <br />\n<br />\n--where is mE beer--<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoB4FJHaPI/AAAAAAAABVM/DgZcuop3v4Q/s1600/topsy1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoB4FJHaPI/AAAAAAAABVM/DgZcuop3v4Q/s1600/topsy1.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Slime ball Edison did this just&nbsp;to prove to the world that Tesla's AC electricity is dangerous . For Tesla had published pictures of himself&nbsp;( not dogs or elephants <span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;) emitting AC 'lightning' from his body. </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For months before that he used to give 25 cents to neighbour hood&nbsp; kids to steal pet dogs and electrocute them with cameras running.&nbsp; He would first&nbsp;toss the poor dogs on the DC grid, the do would yelp and run away-- THEN he would catch the same dog and toss it on the&nbsp;live AC grid and watch them bust into flames , writhe in agony and die.&nbsp; His diabolical way of proving DC is safer than AC.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison could be called the \"Father of Capital Punishment\" &nbsp;.&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">Edison secretly funded the AC Electric chair, though he had nothing to do with AC . It was put to use for the first time on a prisoner by the name of William Kemler. On 6<sup>th</sup> Aug 1890 to prove to the world that AC is unreliable and dangerous to have &nbsp;at home, Edison bribed the prison to use 1000 V and insufficient &nbsp;amperage . &nbsp;<span style=\"color: black;\">Current was passed through Kemmler for 17 seconds. The power was turned off and Kemmler was declared dead &gt; However witnesses noticed Kemmler was still breathing. In the second attempt, Kemmler was shocked with 2,000 volts. Blood vessels under the skin ruptured and bled, all all saw this unfortunate man\u2019s body on fire. Due to the smell of burning flesh, all nauseated and horrified spectators unsuccessfully tried to leave the room. In all, the entire execution took approximately eight minutes. <span class=\"apple-style-span\">A reporter who witnessed it also said it was \"an awful spectacle, far worse than hanging.\" Westinghouse later commented: \"They would have done better using an axe.\"</span> &nbsp;&nbsp;So Edison was indeed successful in this diabolical mission.</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">THIS FORCES ME TO EXPOSE THIS MAN EDISON -- THE&nbsp;DOLLAR WORSHIPPING HERO. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">&nbsp;i would like the Americans to read the following with a open mind , and apply their conscience.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Edison was not an inventor at all.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He was just a manager like Bill Gates. The only difference being Bill Gates is a gentlemen, while Edison was&nbsp;cunning and&nbsp;used to payroll goons with clubs to beat up people who stood in his way and and burn down what he told them to.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Edison was once considered for the Nobel prize to be shared with super genius Nikola Tesla. Tesla refused to share the award with such a ridiculously dumb character, who had NIL foundation in Physics and Maths. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Imagine Bill Gates getting a Nobel prize for doing office administrative work.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The whole world knows that Edison has 1093 Patents to his name. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This is exactly what he was-- a relentless Patent collector -- in a self-delusion of grandeur.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He has NOT added to scientific knowledge at all to this planet-- he was just a innovator using others , NOT an inventor--. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He hardly went to school, his knowledge of Maths was NIL. <span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison began school in Port Huron, Michigan when he was seven. His teacher, the Reverend G. B. Engle considered Thomas to be a daft student.&nbsp;</span> He just did not have the brains to understand Maths. His teacher just told him not to come to school anymore-- unable to tolerate&nbsp;this boys dubious and selfish nature.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Edison didn\u2019t learn to talk until he was four years of age. So he had only three months of formal schooling.&nbsp;At the age of 12 he started business of selling vegetables and newspaper. Soon he started earning good income, such was his business acumen. </span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For saving the life of a station official's child, ( nobody has seen him ) he was rewarded by being taught telegraphy. This proved to be the turning point of this illiterate boys life.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">&nbsp;<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Did he really invent all of those 1,093 inventions he is credited with?&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">NO! </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">He had an army of&nbsp;scientists and innovating engineers on staff at his laboratories in Menlo Park and subsequently in West Orange, NJ.&nbsp; <span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">It was these employees who&nbsp;were responsible for almost all of the patents held in Edison's name.&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">As employees of Edison's company, the employees could not file for the patents in their own names. line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison then protected his stolen idea with a hired band of club welding thugs who would bust up the equipment and the operators of movie cameras, &nbsp;not paying him for use of his patent.&nbsp; One of the reasons that the film capital of the world is in Hollywood is because filmmakers were trying to get away from edison`s club welding thugs who chased them across the country.</span></span> </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoEuzbvTpI/AAAAAAAABVs/5tqT_vM7Sno/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoEuzbvTpI/AAAAAAAABVs/5tqT_vM7Sno/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">Georges Melies made the&nbsp;1902 film : \"Le Voyage Dans La Lune\" (A Trip to the Moon).&nbsp; Melies was one of the foremost filmmakers of his day and his greatest adventure was this film which he poured a lot of money into.&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFfP1EPlI/AAAAAAAABV0/V0OSAoLLUyU/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFfP1EPlI/AAAAAAAABV0/V0OSAoLLUyU/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">The film was finally made and Melies expected it to make a huge amount of money when it was seen in America.&nbsp; It did,&nbsp; &nbsp;but Melies did not see a cent of it because Thomas Edison's agents had bribed a projectionist into letting them borrow it and make hundreds of copies of the film&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">which were then sent to America.</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFlKZyjgI/AAAAAAAABV4/sNm3-3NPZwE/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFlKZyjgI/AAAAAAAABV4/sNm3-3NPZwE/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFoCBsXHI/AAAAAAAABV8/-CBSo7OQf90/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoFoCBsXHI/AAAAAAAABV8/-CBSo7OQf90/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison's film technicians showed these&nbsp;films, all over USA within weeks. Melies never made any money from the film's American showings, and went broke several years later (while Edison made a fortune on the film.)</span></span></span><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Tesla came to America to work first as an employee of Edison.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">His job started as simple&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.topix.com/forum/tech/T3VORFA6ITOIFQD3Q\" target=\"undefined\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; text-decoration: none;\">electrical&nbsp;engineer</span></a>&nbsp;but he quickly demonstrated his extraordinary talent at solving complex problems. &nbsp;Edison asked him to completely redesign the direct current motor and generators, offering him $50,000 (1.5 million in 2010) if he succeeded. Tesla worked day and night to solve the problems and his work led to several patents.&nbsp; When he asked for the promised payment, Edison replied to him, \"Tesla, you don't understand our American humor, do you?\"</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">Edison didn't have the background to understand Tesla's explanation of AC current and whatever little he did understand contradicted what he thought he knew.&nbsp; <span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison was a control freak. Thus when Tesla continued to develop his idea on his own time and Edison got wind of that fact, Edison promptly fired Tesla. </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">After Tesla left Edison he has said \" If Edison had a needle to find in a haystack, he would proceed at once with the diligence of the bee to examine straw after straw until he found the object of his search. ... I was a sorry witness of such doings, knowing that a little theory and calculation would have saved him ninety percent of his labor \" -- it was the anguish of a horse working for a donkey.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\">Edison (who was intimidated by his employee Tesla's genius), is famous for saying &nbsp;\" Genius is 1% inspiration and 99% perspiration\" . &nbsp;He was speaking for himself. What Edison sweated over for one month with an army of scientists -- Tesla could do alone in an minute.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoIQwUhwkI/AAAAAAAABWA/C9w0SiIJX8o/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPoIQwUhwkI/AAAAAAAABWA/C9w0SiIJX8o/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">At the 1893 World\u2019s Fair, Tesla won the contract to light it. Edison denied the use of his bulb, Tesla just made his own.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO8LAMsWqaI/AAAAAAAAAvI/q5q5rd-xUr8/s1600/imagesCAHMQL0L.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO8LAMsWqaI/AAAAAAAAAvI/q5q5rd-xUr8/s1600/imagesCAHMQL0L.jpg\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">Edison&nbsp;had the assistance of 26-year-old Francis <a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/\" name=\"149900.hook\"></a>Upton, a graduate of Princeton University with an M.A. in science. Upton, who joined the laboratory force in December 1878, provided the mathematical and theoretical expertise that Edison himself lacked.&nbsp; <span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Edison himself revealed, \u201cAt the time I experimented on the incandescent lamp I did not understand Ohm's law\"</span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">On his daily walk around the lab grounds, he discovered a bug giving an unusual odor. Edison&nbsp;wrote&nbsp; to a famous scientist, Charles Darwin, about it. All this to prove to the world and hold in posterity that&nbsp; he belonged to the GREATER league of super genuises and honourable gentlemen.-- NOT the mangy tinkerer he was.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">This ruthless &nbsp;and ego-laden man ruined several lives.</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\">He sort of made everything into a popularity contest.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">If any inventor stole patents in this age in USA there would be a&nbsp;federal investigation, and imprisonment.</span></span> </span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\">Some of the ridiculous patents of Edison-- his patrons in the US patents office apparently had no character. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 18px;\">He got so many patents for phonograph--it does not have that many parts!</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;
